لَمَّا سَارَ مُوسَى عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ بِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ بَعْدَ هَلَاكِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَافَوْا ﴿عَلَى قَوْمٍ يَعْكُفُونَ عَلَى أَصْنَامٍ لَهُمْ قَالُوا يَا مُوسَى اجْعَلْ لَنَا إِلَهًا كَمَا لَهُمْ آلِهَةٌ قَالَ إِنَّكُمْ قَوْمٌ تَجْهَلُونَ * إِنَّ هَؤُلاءِ مُتَبَّرٌ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ وَبَاطِلٌ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٣٨، ١٣٩] وَوَاعَدَهُ رَبُّهُ ثَلَاثِينَ لَيْلَةً ثُمَّ أَتْبَعَهَا لَهُ عَشْرًا، فَتَمَّتْ [لَهُ] أَرْبَعِينَ لَيْلَةً، أَيْ: يَصُومُهَا لَيْلًا وَنَهَارًا. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي حَدِيثِ "الْفُتُونِ" بَيَانُ ذَلِكَ. فَسَارَعَ مُوسَى عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ مُبَادِرًا إِلَى الطُّورِ، وَاسْتَخْلَفَ عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ أَخَاهُ هَارُونَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَعْجَلَكَ عَنْ قَوْمِكَ يَا مُوسَى قَالَ هُمْ أُولاءِ عَلَى أَثَرِي﴾ أَيْ: قَادِمُونَ يَنْزِلُونَ قَرِيبًا مِنَ الطُّورِ، ﴿وَعَجِلْتُ إِلَيْكَ رَبِّ لِتَرْضَى﴾ أَيْ: لِتَزْدَادَ عَنِّي رِضًا، ﴿قَالَ فَإِنَّا قَدْ فَتَنَّا قَوْمَكَ مِنْ بَعْدِكَ وَأَضَلَّهُمُ السَّامِرِيُّ﴾ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى نَبَيَّهُ مُوسَى بِمَا كَانَ بَعْدَهُ مِنَ الْحَدَثِ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَعِبَادَتِهِمُ الْعَجَلَ الَّذِي عَمِلَهُ لهم ذلك السَّامِرِيُّ. وَفِي الْكُتُبِ الْإِسْرَائِيلِيَّةِ: أَنَّهُ كَانَ اسْمُهُ هَارُونَ أَيْضًا، وَكَتَبَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لَهُ فِي هَذِهِ الْمُدَّةِ الْأَلْوَاحَ الْمُتَضَمِّنَةَ لِلتَّوْرَاةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَتَبْنَا لَهُ فِي الألْوَاحِ مِنْ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ مَوْعِظَةً وَتَفْصِيلا لِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ فَخُذْهَا بِقُوَّةٍ وَأْمُرْ قَوْمَكَ يَأْخُذُوا بِأَحْسَنِهَا سَأُرِيكُمْ دَارَ الْفَاسِقِينَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٤٥] أَيْ: عَاقِبَةَ الْخَارِجِينَ عَنْ طَاعَتِي الْمُخَالِفِينَ لِأَمْرِي.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَرَجَعَ مُوسَى إِلَى قَوْمِهِ غَضْبَانَ أَسِفًا﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ مَا أَخْبَرَهُ تَعَالَى بِذَلِكَ، فِي غَايَةِ الْغَضَبِ والحَنَق عَلَيْهِمْ، هُوَ فِيمَا هُوَ فِيهِ مِنَ الِاعْتِنَاءِ بِأَمْرِهِمْ، وتَسَلّم التَّوْرَاةِ الَّتِي فِيهَا شَرِيعَتُهُمْ، وَفِيهَا شَرَفٌ لَهُمْ. وَهُمْ قَوْمٌ قَدْ عَبَدُوا غَيْرَ اللَّهِ مَا يَعْلَمُ كُلُّ عَاقِلٍ لَهُ لُبٌّ [وَحَزْمٌ] بُطْلَانَ [مَا هُمْ فِيهِ] وَسَخَافَةَ عُقُولِهِمْ وَأَذْهَانِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا رَجَعَ إِلَيْهِمْ غَضْبَانَ أَسِفًا، وَالْأَسَفُ: شِدَّةُ الْغَضَبِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿غَضْبَانَ أَسِفًا﴾ أَيْ: جَزِعًا. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: ﴿أَسِفًا﴾ أَيْ: حَزِينًا عَلَى مَا صَنَعَ قَوْمُهُ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ.

﴿قَالَ يَا قَوْمِ أَلَمْ يَعِدْكُمْ رَبُّكُمْ وَعْدًا حَسَنًا﴾ أَيْ: أَمَا وَعَدَكُمْ عَلَى لِسَانِي كُلَّ خَيْرٍ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، وَحُسْنَ الْعَاقِبَةِ كَمَا شَاهَدْتُمْ مِنْ نُصْرَتِهُ إِيَّاكُمْ عَلَى عَدُوِّكُمْ، وَإِظْهَارِكُمْ عَلَيْهِ، وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنْ أَيَادِيهِ عِنْدَكُمْ؟ ﴿أَفَطَالَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْعَهْدُ﴾ أَيْ: فِي انْتِظَارِ مَا وَعَدَكُمُ اللَّهُ. وَنِسْيَانِ مَا سَلَفَ مِنْ نِعَمِهِ، وَمَا بِالْعَهْدِ مِنْ قِدَمٍ. ﴿أَمْ أَرَدْتُمْ أَنْ يَحِلَّ عَلَيْكُمْ غَضَبٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ "أَمْ" هَاهُنَا بِمَعْنَى "بَلْ" وَهِيَ لِلْإِضْرَابِ عَنِ الْكَلَامِ الْأَوَّلِ، وَعُدُولٌ إِلَى الثَّانِي، كَأَنَّهُ يَقُولُ: بَلْ أَرَدْتُمْ بِصَنِيعِكُمْ هَذَا أَنْ يَحِلَّ عَلَيْكُمْ غَضَبٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ ﴿فَأَخْلَفْتُمْ مَوْعِدِي * قَالُوا﴾ أَيْ: بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ فِي جَوَابِ مَا أَنَّبَهُمْ مُوسَى وَقَرَّعَهُمْ: ﴿مَا أَخْلَفْنَا مَوْعِدَكَ بِمَلْكِنَا﴾ أَيْ: عَنْ قُدْرَتِنَا وَاخْتِيَارِنَا.

ثُمَّ شَرَعُوا يَعْتَذِرُونَ بِالْعُذْرِ الْبَارِدِ، يُخْبِرُونَهُ عَنْ تَوَرُّعِهِمْ عَمَّا كَانَ بِأَيْدِيهِمْ مِنْ حُلي الْقِبْطِ الَّذِي كَانُوا قَدِ اسْتَعَارُوهُ مِنْهُمْ، حِينَ خَرَجُوا مِنْ مِصْرَ، ﴿فَقَذَفْنَاهَا﴾ أَيْ: أَلْقَيْنَاهَا عَنَّا. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي حَدِيثِ "الْفُتُونِ" أَنَّ هَارُونَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ هُوَ الَّذِي كَانَ أَمَرَهُمْ بِإِلْقَاءِ الْحُلِيِّ فِي حُفْرَةٍ فِيهَا نَارٌ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةِ السُّدِّيّ، عَنْ أَبِي مَالِكٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّمَا أَرَادَ هَارُونُ أَنْ يَجْتَمِعَ الحُلي كُلُّهُ فِي تِلْكَ الْحُفَيْرَةِ وَيُجْعَلَ حَجَرًا وَاحِدًا. حَتَّى إِذَا رَجَعَ مُوسَى يَرَى فِيهِ مَا يَشَاءُ. ثُمَّ جَاءَ [بَعْدَ] ذَلِكَ السَّامِرِيُّ فَأَلْقَى عَلَيْهَا تِلْكَ الْقَبْضَةَ الَّتِي أَخَذَهَا مِنْ أَثَرِ الرَّسُولِ، وَسَأَلَ هَارُونَ أَنْ يَدْعُوَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَسْتَجِيبَ لَهُ فِي دَعْوَتِهِ، فَدَعَا لَهُ هَارُونُ -وَهُوَ لَا يَعْلَمُ مَا يُرِيدُ -فَأُجِيبَ لَهُ فَقَالَ السَّامِرِيُّ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ: أَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَكُونَ عِجْلًا. فَكَانَ عِجْلًا لَهُ خُوار، أَيْ: صَوْتٌ، اسْتِدْرَاجًا وَإِمْهَالًا وَمِحْنَةً وَاخْتِبَارًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا: ﴿فَكَذَلِكَ أَلْقَى السَّامِرِيُّ * فَأَخْرَجَ لَهُمْ عِجْلا جَسَدًا لَهُ خُوَارٌ﴾

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ البَخْتَريّ حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بن هارون أخبرنا حَمَّاد عَنْ سِمَاكٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّ هَارُونَ مَرَّ بِالسَّامِرِيِّ وَهُوَ يَنْحِتُ الْعِجْلَ، فَقَالَ لَهُ: مَا تَصْنَعُ؟ فَقَالَ: أَصْنَعُ مَا يَضُرُّ وَلَا يَنْفَعُ فَقَالَ هَارُونُ: اللَّهُمَّ أَعْطِهِ مَا سَأَلَ عَلَى مَا فِي نَفْسِهِ وَمَضَى هَارُونُ، فَقَالَ السَّامِرِيُّ: اللَّهُمَّ إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ أَنْ يَخُور فَخَار، فَكَانَ إِذَا خَارَ سَجَدُوا لَهُ، وَإِذَا خَارَ رَفَعُوا رُؤُوسَهُمْ.

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ عَنْ حَمَّادٍ وَقَالَ: [أَعْمَلُ] مَا يَنْفَعُ وَلَا يَضُرُّ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: كَانَ يَخُورُ وَيَمْشِي.

فَقَالُوا -أَيِ: الضُّلال مِنْهُمُ، الَّذِينَ افْتُتِنُوا بِالْعِجْلِ وَعَبَدُوهُ -: ﴿هَذَا إِلَهُكُمْ وَإِلَهُ مُوسَى فَنَسِيَ﴾ أَيْ: نَسِيَهُ هَاهُنَا، وَذَهَبَ يَتَطَلَّبُهُ. كَذَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي حَدِيثِ "الْفُتُونِ" عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَبِهِ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ.

وَقَالَ سِماك عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَنَسِيَ﴾ أَيْ: نَسِيَ أَنْ يُذَكِّرَكُمْ أَنَّ هَذَا إِلَهُكُمْ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ حَكِيمِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فَقَالُوا: ﴿هَذَا إِلَهُكُمْ وَإِلَهُ مُوسَى﴾ قَالَ: فَعَكَفُوا عَلَيْهِ وَأَحَبُّوهُ حُبًّا لَمْ يُحِبُّوا شَيْئًا قَطُّ يَعْنِي مِثْلَهُ، يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: ﴿فَنَسِيَ﴾ أَيْ: تَرَكَ مَا كَانَ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْإِسْلَامِ يَعْنِي: السَّامِرِيَّ.

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى رَدًّا عَلَيْهِمْ، وَتَقْرِيعًا لَهُمْ، وَبَيَانًا لِفَضِيحَتِهِمْ وَسَخَافَةِ عُقُولِهِمْ فِيمَا ذَهَبُوا إِلَيْهِ: ﴿أَفَلا يَرَوْنَ أَلا يَرْجِعُ إِلَيْهِمْ قَوْلا وَلا يَمْلِكُ لَهُمْ ضَرًّا وَلا نَفْعًا﴾ أَيِ: الْعَجَلُ ﴿أَفَلا يَرَوْنَ﴾ أَنَّهُ لَا يُجِيبُهُمْ إِذَا سَأَلُوهُ، وَلَا إِذَا خَاطَبُوهُ، ﴿وَلا يَمْلِكُ لَهُمْ ضَرًّا وَلا نَفْعًا﴾ أَيْ: فِي دُنْيَاهُمْ وَلَا فِي أُخْرَاهُمْ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ لَا وَاللَّهِ مَا كَانَ خُوَارُهُ إِلَّا أَنْ يَدْخُلَ الريح في دبره فيخرج فِيهِ، فَيُسْمَعَ لَهُ صَوْتٌ.

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي مُتُونِ الْحَدِيثِ عَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ: أَنَّ هَذَا الْعَجَلَ اسْمُهُ بَهْمُوتُ.

وَحَاصِلُ مَا اعْتَذَرَ بِهِ هَؤُلَاءِ الْجَهَلَةُ أَنَّهُمْ تَوَرَّعُوا عَنْ زِينَةِ الْقِبْطِ، فَأَلْقَوْهَا عَنْهُمْ، وَعَبَدُوا الْعِجْلَ. فَتَوَرَّعُوا عَنِ الْحَقِيرِ وَفَعَلُوا الْأَمْرَ الْكَبِيرَ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الصَّحِيحِ عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ: أَنَّهُ سَأَلَهُ رَجُلٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْعِرَاقِ عَنْ دَمِ الْبَعُوضِ إِذَا أَصَابَ الثَّوْبَ -يَعْنِي: هَلْ يُصَلِّي فِيهِ أَمْ لَا؟ -فَقَالَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: انْظُرُوا إِلَى أَهْلِ الْعِرَاقِ، قَتَلُوا ابْنَ بِنْتِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ -يعني: الحسين -وهم يسألون عن دم البعوض؟ .

---

## 20:90-91 — verses 90-91 (shared commentary)

### Translation

الله تعالى يخبر عما كان من نهي هارون، عليه السلام، لهم عن عبادة العجل، وإخباره إياهم أن هذا إنما هو فتنة لكم، {وَإِنَّ رَبَّكُمُ الرَّحْمَنُ} الذي خلق كل شيء فقدره تقديرا، ذو العرش المجيد، الفعال لما يريد، {فَاتَّبِعُونِي} أي: فيما آمركم به، واتركوا ما أنهاكم عنه.

Below is my translation:

The Almighty relates what happened when Harun (peace be upon him) forbade them from worshipping the calf, and informed them that this was merely a trial for them: {And indeed your Lord is the Most Merciful (al-Rahman)}, who created everything and determined it with precise measure, Possessor of the glorious Throne, the One who does whatever He wills, {so follow me}, meaning: in what I command you, and abandon what I forbid you from.

{They said, "We will never cease to worship it until Musa returns to us"}, meaning: we will not abandon its worship until we hear what Musa has to say about it. They opposed Harun in this, fought against him, and nearly killed him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا كَانَ مِنْ نَهْي هَارُونَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَهُمْ عَنْ عِبَادَةِ الْعِجْلِ، وَإِخْبَارِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ: إِنَّمَا هَذَا فِتْنَةٌ لَكُمْ ﴿وَإِنَّ رَبَّكُمُ الرَّحْمَنُ﴾ الَّذِي خَلَقَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ فَقَدَّرَهُ تَقْدِيرًا، ذُو الْعَرْشِ الْمَجِيدِ، الْفَعَّالُ لِمَا يُرِيدُ ﴿فَاتَّبِعُونِي﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا آمُرُكُمْ بِهِ، وَاتْرُكُوا مَا أَنْهَاكُمْ عَنْهُ.

﴿قَالُوا لَنْ نَبْرَحَ عَلَيْهِ عَاكِفِينَ حَتَّى يَرْجِعَ إِلَيْنَا مُوسَى﴾ أَيْ: لَا نَتْرُكَ عِبَادَتَهُ حَتَّى نَسْمَعَ كَلَامَ مُوسَى فِيهِ. وَخَالَفُوا هَارُونَ فِي ذَلِكَ وَحَارَبُوهُ وَكَادُوا أَنْ يَقْتُلُوهُ.

---

## 20:92-94 — verses 92-94 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He says, reporting about Moses (peace be upon him), when he returned to his people and saw what great matter had occurred among them, he became filled with rage at that. He threw down what he had in his hand, the divine tablets, and seized his brother's head, pulling him toward himself. We have already given a full account of this in Surat al-A'raf, and mentioned there the hadith "the report is not like witnessing with one's own eyes."

He began to blame his brother Aaron, saying: {What prevented you, when you saw them going astray, from following me?} meaning: from informing me of this matter as soon as it occurred. {Have you then disobeyed my command?} meaning: regarding what I had entrusted to you beforehand, which is His saying: {Take my place among my people, set things right, and do not follow the way of those who cause corruption} [al-A'raf: 142]. He said: {O son of my mother}, being gentle with him by mentioning the mother, even though he was his full brother from both parents, because mentioning the mother here carries more tenderness and is more effective in conveying compassion and affection. This is why he said: {O son of my mother, do not seize me by my beard or by my head. I feared that you would say, "You have caused division among the Children of Israel and did not wait for my word."}

This is an excuse offered by Aaron to Moses concerning the reason for his delay in following him, in that he had not caught up with him to inform him of what had happened in this grave affair. He said: {I feared} that if I followed you and informed you of this, you would say to me: why did you leave them alone and cause division among them? {and did not wait for my word}, meaning: and did not observe what I had commanded you when I appointed you as my successor over them.

Ibn Abbas said: Aaron held Moses in awe and was obedient to him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ مُخْبِرًا عَنْ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، حِينَ رَجَعَ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، فَرَأَى مَا قَدْ حَدَثَ فِيهِمْ مِنَ الْأَمْرِ الْعَظِيمِ، فَامْتَلَأَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ غَيْظًا، وَأَلْقَى مَا كَانَ فِي يَدِهِ مِنَ الْأَلْوَاحِ الْإِلَهِيَّةِ، وَأَخَذَ بِرَأْسِ أَخِيهِ يَجُرُّهُ إِلَيْهِ، وَقَدْ قَدَّمْنَا فِي "الْأَعْرَافِ" بَسْطَ ذَلِكَ، وَذَكَرْنَا هُنَاكَ حَدِيثَ "لَيْسَ الْخَبَرُ كَالْمُعَايَنَةِ".

وَشَرَعَ يَلُومُ أَخَاهُ هَارُونَ فَقَالَ: ﴿مَا مَنَعَكَ إِذْ رَأَيْتَهُمْ ضَلُّوا * أَلا تَتَّبِعَنِ﴾ أَيْ: فَتُخْبِرَنِي بِهَذَا الْأَمْرِ أَوَّلَ مَا وَقَعَ ﴿أَفَعَصَيْتَ أَمْرِي﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا كُنْتُ تَقَدَّمْتُ إِلَيْكَ، وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿اخْلُفْنِي فِي قَوْمِي وَأَصْلِحْ وَلا تَتَّبِعْ سَبِيلَ الْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٤٢] . قَالَ: ﴿يَا ابْنَ أُمَّ﴾ تَرَفَّقَ لَهُ بِذِكْرِ الْأُمِّ مَعَ أَنَّهُ شَقِيقُهُ لِأَبَوَيْهِ؛ لِأَنَّ ذِكْرَ الْأُمِّ هَاهُنَا أَرَقُّ وَأَبْلَغُ، أَيْ: فِي الْحُنُوِّ وَالْعَطْفِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَا ابْنَ أُمَّ لَا تَأْخُذْ بِلِحْيَتِي وَلا بِرَأْسِي إِنِّي خَشِيتُ أَنْ تَقُولَ فَرَّقْتَ بَيْنَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ وَلَمْ تَرْقُبْ قَوْلِي﴾ .

هَذَا اعْتِذَارٌ مِنْ هَارُونَ عِنْدَ مُوسَى فِي سَبَبِ تَأَخُّرِهِ عَنْهُ، حَيْثُ لَمْ يَلْحَقْهُ فَيُخْبِرْهُ بِمَا كَانَ مِنْ هَذَا الْخَطْبِ الْجَسِيمِ قَالَ ﴿إِنِّي خَشِيتُ﴾ أَنْ أَتْبَعَكَ فَأُخْبِرَكَ بِهَذَا، فَتَقُولَ لِي: لِمَ تَرَكْتَهُمْ وَحْدَهُمْ وَفَرَّقْتَ بَيْنَهُمْ ﴿وَلَمْ تَرْقُبْ قَوْلِي﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا رَاعَيْتَ مَا أَمَرْتُكَ بِهِ حَيْثُ اسْتَخْلَفْتُكَ فِيهِمْ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَكَانَ هَارُونُ هَائِبًا لَهُ مُطِيعًا.

---

## 20:95-98 — verses 95-98 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Musa (peace be upon him) says to al-Samiri: "What made you do what you did? What was it that came upon you that made you do what you did?"

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Hakim ibn Jubayr, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: al-Samiri was a man from the people of Bajarma, and he was from a people who worshipped cattle. The love of cattle-worship was in his heart, and he had outwardly professed Islam while among the Children of Israel. The name of al-Samiri was Musa ibn Zufar.

In another report from Ibn Abbas: he was from Kirman.

Qatada said: he was from a village called Samarra.

{He said, "I saw what they did not see"} that is, "I saw Jibril when he came for the destruction of Pharaoh," {so I took a handful from the track of the messenger} that is, from the track of his horse. This is what is well known among many, or most, of the commentators.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: When Jibril, peace be upon him, descended and ascended with Musa to the heaven, al-Samiri alone among the people caught sight of him, and he took a handful from the track of the horse. He said: Jibril carried Musa behind him, until when he drew near the gate of heaven, he ascended, and Allah wrote the Tablets while Musa heard the creaking of the pens on the Tablets. When Allah informed him that his people had been led into trial after him, he said: Musa descended and took the calf and burned it. This is gharib (a singular report). Mujahid said regarding {so I took a handful from the track of the messenger}: from beneath the hoof of the horse of Jibril. He said: the handful is a fistful, and the handful is with the fingertips.

Mujahid said: al-Samiri "cast," meaning he threw what was in his hand onto the ornaments of the Children of Israel, and it was cast into the form of a calf, a body that had a lowing sound like the rushing of wind within it, and that was its lowing.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Ikrima, that al-Samiri saw the messenger (Jibril), and it was cast into his mind that if he took a handful from the track of this horse and threw it into something, saying to it "Be," it would be. So he took a handful from the track of the messenger, and his fingers dried tight upon the handful. When Musa went for the appointed meeting, and the Children of Israel had borrowed the ornaments of Pharaoh's people, al-Samiri said to them: What has befallen you is only because of these ornaments, so gather them together. They gathered them, and lit a fire over them, and they melted. Al-Samiri saw this, and it was cast into his mind that if he threw this handful into it and said "Be," it would be. So he threw the handful and said "Be," and it became a calf that had a lowing sound, and he said, {"This is your god and the god of Musa."}

For this reason he said, {so I cast it}, that is, "I threw it along with those who threw," {and thus my soul enticed me}, that is, it made it seem good to it and it was pleased with it at that time.

{He said, "Then go, for indeed for you in this life is that you shall say, 'No touching'"} that is, just as you took and touched what was not permissible to take or touch from the track of the messenger, so your punishment in this world is that you shall say "No touching," meaning: you shall not touch people, nor shall they touch you.

{And indeed for you is an appointed time that you shall not fail to keep} that is, on the Day of Resurrection, {you shall not fail to keep} meaning there is no escape from it for you.

Qatada said regarding {that you shall say, "No touching"}: it was a punishment for them, and their remnants today say, "No touching."

Regarding His saying {And indeed for you is an appointed time that you shall not fail to keep}, al-Hasan, Qatada, and Abu Nahik said: it means you shall not be absent from it.

Regarding His saying {And look at your god}, meaning your object of worship, {which you have persisted in devotion to} that is, you remained constant in worshipping it, meaning the calf, {we will surely burn it}. Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas, and al-Suddi: he filed it down with files and threw it into the fire.

Qatada said: the calf turned from gold into flesh and blood, so he burned it with fire, then he threw it, meaning its ashes, into the sea. For this reason He said, {then We will surely scatter it into the sea, a total scattering}.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: when Musa hastened to his Lord, al-Samiri set about gathering what he could of the ornaments of the women of the Children of Israel, then he shaped it into a calf. He said: Musa then took the calf and applied files to it, filing it down, while standing on the bank of a river, and no one who had worshipped the calf drank from that water without his face turning yellow like gold. They said to Musa: What is our repentance? He said: that some of you kill others.

This is what al-Suddi likewise said, and this has already been discussed at length in the commentary on Surat al-Baqara, and then in the hadith of "al-Futun" (the trials).

Regarding His saying {Your god is only Allah, He besides whom there is no other god, He encompasses all things in knowledge}: Musa, peace be upon him, says to them: This is not your god, your god is only Allah, He besides whom there is no other god, that is, none besides Him deserves this from His servants, and worship is not fitting for anyone but Him, for everything is in need of Him, a servant to its Lord.

Regarding His saying {He encompasses all things in knowledge}: it is set in the accusative as a specifier, meaning He has knowledge of all things: {He has encompassed all things in knowledge} [al-Talaq: 12], {and has numbered all things in number} [al-Jinn: 28], so {not even the weight of an atom escapes Him} [Saba: 3], {and not a leaf falls but that He knows it, nor a grain in the darkness of the earth, nor anything moist or dry, but that it is in a clear register} [al-An'am: 59], {and there is no creature on the earth but that its provision is upon Allah, and He knows its dwelling place and its resting place, all is in a clear register} [Hud: 6]. The verses on this matter are exceedingly many.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لِلسَّامِرِيِّ: مَا حَمَلَكَ عَلَى مَا صَنَعْتَ؟ وَمَا الَّذِي عَرَضَ لَكَ حَتَّى فَعَلْتَ مَا فَعَلْتَ؟

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ حَكِيمِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ السَّامِرِيُّ رَجُلًا مِنْ أَهْلِ بَاجَرْمَا، وَكَانَ مَنْ قَوْمٍ يَعْبُدُونَ الْبَقَرَ، وَكَانَ حُبُّ عِبَادَةِ الْبَقَرِ فِي نَفْسِهِ، وَكَانَ قَدْ أَظْهَرَ الْإِسْلَامَ مَعَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. وَكَانَ اسْمَ السَّامِرِيِّ: مُوسَى بْنُ ظُفَرٍ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: [أَنَّهُ] كَانَ مِنْ كَرْمَانَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كَانَ مِنْ قَرْيَةٍ اسْمُهَا سَامَرَّا.

﴿قَالَ بَصُرْتُ بِمَا لَمْ يَبْصُرُوا بِهِ﴾ أَيْ: رَأَيْتُ جِبْرِيلَ حِينَ جَاءَ لِهَلَاكِ فِرْعَوْنَ، ﴿فَقَبَضْتُ قَبْضَةً مِنْ أَثَرِ الرَّسُولِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَثَرِ فَرَسِهِ. وَهَذَا هُوَ الْمَشْهُورُ عِنْدَ كَثِيرٍ مِنَ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ أَوْ أَكْثَرِهِمْ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عمار بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، أَخْبَرَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُوسَى، أَخْبَرَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ السُّدِّيِّ، عَنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ عُمَارَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِنَّ جِبْرِيلَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَمَّا نَزَلَ فَصَعِدَ بِمُوسَى إِلَى السَّمَاءِ، بُصُرَ بِهِ السَّامِرِيُّ مِنْ بَيْنِ النَّاسِ، فَقَبَضَ قَبْضَةً مِنْ أَثَرِ الْفَرَسِ قَالَ: وَحَمَلَ جِبْرِيلُ مُوسَى خَلْفَهُ، حَتَّى إِذَا دَنَا مِنْ بَابِ السَّمَاءِ، صَعِدَ وَكَتَبَ اللَّهُ الْأَلْوَاحَ وَهُوَ يَسْمَعُ صَرِيرَ الْأَقْلَامِ فِي الْأَلْوَاحِ. فَلَمَّا أَخْبَرَهُ أَنَّ قَوْمَهُ قَدْ فُتِنُوا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ قَالَ: نَزَلَ مُوسَى، فَأَخَذَ الْعِجْلَ فَأَحْرَقَهُ. غَرِيبٌ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿فَقَبَضْتُ قَبْضَةً مِنْ أَثَرِ الرَّسُولِ﴾ قَالَ: مِنْ تَحْتِ حَافِرِ فَرَسِ جِبْرِيلَ، قَالَ: وَالْقَبْضَةُ مِلْءُ الْكَفِّ، وَالْقَبْضَةُ بِأَطْرَافِ الْأَصَابِعِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: نَبَذَ السَّامِرِيُّ، أَيْ: أَلْقَى مَا كَانَ فِي يَدِهِ عَلَى حِلْيَةِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَانْسَبَكَ عِجْلًا جَسَدًا لَهُ خُوار حَفِيفُ الرِّيحِ فِيهِ، فَهُوَ خُوَارُهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يحيى، أخبرنا علي بن الْمَدِينِيِّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ زُرَيْع، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَارَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا عِكْرِمَةُ؛ أَنَّ السَّامِرِيَّ رَأَى الرَّسُولَ، فَأُلْقِيَ فِي رَوْعِهِ أَنَّكَ إِنْ أَخَذْتَ مِنْ أَثَرِ هَذَا الْفَرَسِ قَبْضَةً فَأَلْقَيْتَهَا فِي شَيْءٍ، فَقُلْتُ لَهُ: "كُنْ فَكَانَ" فَقَبَضَ قَبْضَةً مِنْ أَثَرِ الرَّسُولِ، فَيَبِسَتْ أَصَابِعُهُ عَلَى الْقَبْضَةِ، فَلَمَّا ذَهَبَ مُوسَى لِلْمِيقَاتِ وَكَانَ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ اسْتَعَارُوا حُلِيَّ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ، فَقَالَ لَهُمُ السَّامِرِيُّ: إِنَّمَا أَصَابَكُمْ مِنْ أَجْلِ هَذَا الْحُلِيِّ، فَاجْمَعُوهُ. فَجَمَعُوهُ، فَأَوْقَدُوا عَلَيْهِ، فَذَابَ، فَرَآهُ السَّامِرِيُّ فَأُلْقِيَ فِي رُوعِهِ أَنَّكَ لَوْ قَذَفْتَ هَذِهِ الْقَبْضَةَ فِي هَذِهِ فَقُلْتَ: "كُنْ" كَانَ. فَقَذَفَ الْقَبْضَةَ وَقَالَ: "كُنْ"، فَكَانَ عِجْلًا لَهُ خُوَارٌ، فَقَالَ: ﴿هَذَا إِلَهُكُمْ وَإِلَهُ مُوسَى﴾ .

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَنَبَذْتُهَا﴾ أَيْ: أَلْقَيْتُهَا مَعَ مَنْ أَلْقَى، ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ سَوَّلَتْ لِي نَفْسِي﴾ أَيْ: حَسَّنَتْهُ وَأَعْجَبَهَا إِذْ ذَاكَ.

﴿قَالَ فَاذْهَبْ فَإِنَّ لَكَ فِي الْحَيَاةِ أَنْ تَقُولَ لَا مِسَاسَ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا أَخَذْتَ ومَسَسْتَ مَا لَمْ يَكُنْ أَخْذُهُ وَمَسُّهُ مِنْ أَثَرِ الرَّسُولِ، فَعُقُوبَتُكَ فِي الدُّنْيَا أَنْ تَقُولَ: "لَا مِسَاسَ" أَيْ: لَا تَمَاسُّ النَّاسَ وَلَا يَمَسُّونَكَ.

﴿وَإِنَّ لَكَ مَوْعِدًا﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿لَنْ تُخْلَفَهُ﴾ أَيْ: لَا مَحِيدَ لَكَ عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿أَنْ تَقُولَ لَا مِسَاسَ﴾ قَالَ: عُقُوبَةٌ لَهُمْ، وَبَقَايَاهُمُ الْيَوْمَ يَقُولُونَ: لَا مِسَاسَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ لَكَ مَوْعِدًا لَنْ تُخْلَفَهُ﴾ قَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَأَبُو نَهِيك: لَنْ تَغِيبَ عَنْهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَانْظُرْ إِلَى إِلَهِكَ﴾ أَيْ: مَعْبُودِكَ، ﴿الَّذِي ظَلْتَ عَلَيْهِ عَاكِفًا﴾ أَيْ: أَقَمْتَ عَلَى عِبَادَتِهِ، يَعْنِي: الْعِجْلَ ﴿لَنُحَرِّقَنَّهُ﴾ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالسُّدِّيِّ: سَحَله بِالْمَبَارِدِ، وَأَلْقَاهُ عَلَى النَّارِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: اسْتَحَالَ الْعِجْلُ مِنَ الذَّهَبِ لَحْمًا وَدَمًا، فَحَرَقَهُ بِالنَّارِ، ثُمَّ أَلْقَاهُ، أَيْ: رَمَادَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ثُمَّ لَنَنْسِفَنَّهُ فِي الْيَمِّ نَسْفًا﴾ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ رَجَاءٍ، أَنْبَأَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عُمَارَةَ بْنِ عَبْدٍ وَأَبِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِنَّ مُوسَى لَمَّا تَعَجَّلَ إِلَى رَبِّهِ، عَمَدَ السَّامِرِيُّ فَجَمَعَ مَا قَدَرَ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ حُلِيِّ نِسَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، ثُمَّ صَوَّرَهُ عِجْلًا قَالَ: فَعَمَدَ مُوسَى إِلَى الْعِجْلِ، فَوَضَعَ عَلَيْهِ الْمَبَارِدَ، فَبَرَدَهُ بِهَا، وَهُوَ عَلَى شَطِّ نَهْرٍ، فَلَمْ يَشْرَبْ أَحَدٌ مِنْ ذَلِكَ الْمَاءِ مِمَّنْ كَانَ يَعْبُدُ الْعِجْلَ إِلَّا اصْفَرَّ وَجْهُهُ مِثْلَ الذَّهَبِ. فَقَالُوا لِمُوسَى: مَا تَوْبَتُنَا ؟ قَالَ: يَقْتُلُ بَعْضُكُمْ بَعْضًا.

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي تَفْسِيرِ سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ" ثُمَّ فِي حَدِيثِ "الْفُتُونِ" بَسْطُ ذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّمَا إِلَهُكُمُ اللَّهُ الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ [وَسِعَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا﴾ يَقُولُ لَهُمْ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: لَيْسَ هَذَا إِلَهَكُمْ، إِنَّمَا إِلَهُكُمُ اللَّهُ الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ] أَيْ: لَا يَسْتَحِقُّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى الْعِبَادِ إِلَّا هُوَ، وَلَا تَنْبَغِي الْعِبَادَةُ إِلَّا لَهُ، فَإِنَّ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ فَقِيرٌ إِلَيْهِ، عَبْدٌ لِرَبِّهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَسِعَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا﴾ نُصِبَ عَلَى التَّمْيِيزِ، أَيْ: هُوَ عَالِمٌ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ، ﴿أَحَاطَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا﴾ [الطَّلَاقِ: ١٢] ، ﴿وَأَحْصَى كُلَّ شَيْءٍ عَدَدًا﴾ [الْجِنِّ: ٢٨] ، فَلَا ﴿يَعْزُبُ عَنْهُ مِثْقَالُ ذَرَّةٍ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٣] ، ﴿وَمَا تَسْقُطُ مِنْ وَرَقَةٍ إِلا يَعْلَمُهَا وَلا حَبَّةٍ فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الأرْضِ وَلا رَطْبٍ وَلا يَابِسٍ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٥٩] ، ﴿وَمَا مِنْ دَابَّةٍ فِي الأرْضِ إِلا عَلَى اللَّهِ رِزْقُهَا وَيَعْلَمُ مُسْتَقَرَّهَا وَمُسْتَوْدَعَهَا كُلٌّ فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٦] وَالْآيَاتُ فِي هذا كثيرة جدًّا.

---

## 20:99-101 — verses 99-101 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says to His Prophet Muhammad ﷺ: just as We related to you the account of Musa, and what took place between him and Fir'awn and his troops exactly as it happened and in accordance with the actual event, so too do We relate to you the past accounts just as they occurred, without addition or diminishment. This is the meaning of {and We have given you from Us} that is, from Our presence, {a remembrance}, which is the Mighty Qur'an, the one {which falsehood cannot approach from before it or from behind it, a revelation from One who is Wise, Praiseworthy} [Fussilat: 42]. No prophet among the prophets, from when they were sent until they were sealed with Muhammad ﷺ, was given a book like it, nor more complete than it, nor more comprehensive of the accounts of what preceded, the accounts of what is to come, and the judgment for deciding between people. That is why the Almighty said: {whoever turns away from it}, meaning: denies it and turns away from following it, whether in obligation or in seeking, and seeks guidance elsewhere, then Allah will lead him astray and guide him to the middle of the Blazing Fire. That is why He said: {whoever turns away from it will indeed carry on the Day of Resurrection a burden}, meaning: a sin, just as the Almighty said: {and whoever disbelieves in it among the factions, the Fire is his promised place} [Hud: 17].

This is general, applying to everyone whom the Qur'an reaches, whether Arab or non-Arab, People of the Book or others, just as the Almighty said: {that I may warn you thereby, and whomever it reaches} [al-An'am: 19]. So everyone whom the Qur'an reaches, it serves as a warner and a caller to him. Whoever follows it is guided, and whoever opposes it and turns away from it goes astray and is made wretched in this world, and the Fire is his promised place on the Day of Resurrection. That is why He said: {whoever turns away from it will indeed carry on the Day of Resurrection a burden, abiding therein forever}, meaning: they will have no escape from it and no release, {and evil it is for them on the Day of Resurrection as a burden}, meaning: how evil is their burden.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ: كَمَا قَصَصْنَا عَلَيْكَ خَبَرَ مُوسَى، وَمَا جَرَى لَهُ مَعَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَجُنُودِهِ عَلَى الْجَلِيَّةِ وَالْأَمْرِ الْوَاقِعِ، كَذَلِكَ نَقُصُّ عَلَيْكَ الْأَخْبَارَ الْمَاضِيَةَ كَمَا وَقَعَتْ مِنْ غَيْرِ زِيَادَةٍ وَلَا نَقْصٍ، هَذَا ﴿وَقَدْ آتَيْنَاكَ مِنْ لَدُنَّا﴾ أَيْ: عِنْدِنَا ﴿ذِكْرًا﴾ وَهُوَ الْقُرْآنُ الْعَظِيمُ، الذِي ﴿لَا يَأْتِيهِ الْبَاطِلُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَلا مِنْ خَلْفِهِ تَنزيلٌ مِنْ حَكِيمٍ حَمِيدٍ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٤٢] ، الَّذِي لَمْ يُعْطَ نَبِيٌّ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ [مُنْذُ بُعِثُوا إِلَى أَنْ خُتِمُوا] بِمُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ تَسْلِيمًا، كِتَابًا مِثْلَهُ وَلَا أَكْمَلَ مِنْهُ، وَلَا أَجْمَعَ لِخَبَرِ مَا سَبَقَ وَخَبَرِ مَا هُوَ كَائِنٌ، وَحُكْمِ الْفَصْلِ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ مِنْهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَنْ أَعْرَضَ عَنْهُ﴾ أَيْ: كَذَّبَ بِهِ وَأَعْرَضَ عَنِ اتِّبَاعِهِ أَمْرًا وَطَلَبًا، وَابْتَغَى الْهُدَى فِي غَيْرِهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يُضِلُّهُ وَيَهْدِيهِ إِلَى سَوَاءِ الْجَحِيمِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَنْ أَعْرَضَ عَنْهُ فَإِنَّهُ يَحْمِلُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وِزْرًا﴾ أَيْ: إِثْمًا، كَمَا قَالَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِهِ مِنَ الأحْزَابِ فَالنَّارُ مَوْعِدُهُ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٧] .

وَهَذَا عَامٌّ فِي كُلِّ مَنْ بَلَغَهُ الْقُرْآنُ مِنَ الْعَرَبِ وَالْعَجَمِ، أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ وَغَيْرُهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لأنْذِرَكُمْ بِهِ وَمَنْ بَلَغَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٩] . فَكُلُّ مَنْ بَلَغَهُ الْقُرْآنُ فَهُوَ نَذِيرٌ لَهُ وَدَاعٍ، فَمَنِ اتَّبَعَهُ هُدِيَ، وَمَنْ خَالَفَهُ وَأَعْرَضَ عَنْهُ ضَلَّ وَشَقِيَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَالنَّارُ مَوْعِدُهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَنْ أَعْرَضَ عَنْهُ فَإِنَّهُ يَحْمِلُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وِزْرًا * خَالِدِينَ فِيهِ﴾ أَيْ: لَا مَحِيد لَهُمْ عَنْهُ وَلَا انْفِكَاكَ ﴿وَسَاءَ لَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ حِمْلا﴾ أَيْ: بِئْسَ الْحِمْلُ حِمْلُهُمْ.

---

## 20:102-104 — verses 102-104 (shared commentary)

### Translation

It is established in the hadith that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked about the Sur (Trumpet), and he said: "It is a horn that is blown into."

It has come in the hadith of "the Sur," through the narration of Abu Hurayrah: that it is a mighty horn, its circumference being the measure of the heavens and the earth, and that Israfil (peace be upon him) blows into it. And it has come in the hadith: "How can I feel at ease when the holder of the horn has already put it to his lips, bent his forehead, and is waiting to be given permission?" They said: O Messenger of Allah, what shall we say? He said: "Say: Sufficient for us is Allah, and He is the best disposer of affairs; upon Allah we place our trust."

Concerning His saying, {And We will gather the criminals on that Day, blue-eyed}: it has been said that its meaning is that their eyes will be blue from the intensity of the terrors they are experiencing.

{Whispering among themselves}: Ibn Abbas said, meaning they murmur secretly among themselves, that is, some of them say to others: {You remained not except ten [days]},

meaning: in the worldly abode, your stay there was but a little, ten days or thereabouts.

Allah, Exalted is He, said: {We are most knowing of what they say}, that is, during their whispered conversation among themselves, {when the most exemplary of them in conduct will say}, meaning the most sound-minded and complete in judgment among them, {You remained not except one day}, that is, because of the shortness of the duration of the worldly life in their own estimation on the Day of Return. For the whole of this worldly life, however much its times recurred and its nights and days succeeded one another, and its hours, seems like a single day. This is why the duration of worldly life will seem so short on the Day of Resurrection. Their purpose in saying this was to fend off the establishment of the proof against them on account of the shortness of the period. This is why Allah, Exalted is He, said: {And on the Day the Hour appears, the criminals will swear they had remained but an hour. Thus were they deluded. But those who were given knowledge and faith will say: You had remained, according to the decree of Allah, until the Day of Resurrection, and this is the Day of Resurrection, but you did not know} [al-Rum: 55, 56]. And He, Exalted is He, said: {Did We not grant you life long enough for whoever would remember to remember therein, and the warner came to you? So taste [the punishment], for the wrongdoers have no helper} [Fatir: 37]. And He, Exalted is He, said: {He will say: How long did you remain on earth in number of years? They will say: We remained a day or part of a day, so ask those who keep count. He will say: You remained not except a little, if only you had known} [al-Muminun: 112-114], meaning: your stay there was indeed but a little, and if only you had known, you would have preferred what endures over what perishes. But instead you conducted yourselves and conducted yourselves badly, giving precedence to the present, perishing thing over the everlasting, abiding one.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ثَبَتَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ سُئِل عَنِ الصُّور، فَقَالَ: "قَرنٌ يُنفَخ فِيهِ" .

وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي حَدِيثِ "الصُّورِ" مِنْ رِوَايَةِ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ: أَنَّهُ قَرْنٌ عَظِيمٌ، الدَّارة مِنْهُ بِقَدْرِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ، يَنْفُخُ فِيهِ إِسْرَافِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ. وَجَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "كَيْفَ أنعَمُ وَصَاحِبُ القَرْن قَدِ الْتَقَمَ القَرْن، وَحَنَى جَبْهَتَهُ، وَانْتَظَرَ أَنْ يُؤْذَنَ لَهُ" فَقَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ نَقُولُ؟ قَالَ: "قُولُوا: حَسْبُنَا اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ، عَلَى اللَّهِ تَوَكَّلْنَا" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنَحْشُرُ الْمُجْرِمِينَ يَوْمَئِذٍ زُرْقًا﴾ قِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ زُرْق الْعُيُونِ مِنْ شِدَّةِ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْأَهْوَالِ.

﴿يَتَخَافَتُونَ بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَتَسَارُّونَ بَيْنَهُمْ، أَيْ: يَقُولُ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ: ﴿إِنْ لَبِثْتُمْ إِلا عَشْرًا﴾

أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا، لَقَدْ كَانَ لُبْثُكُمْ فِيهَا قَلِيلًا عَشَرَةُ أَيْامٍ أَوْ نَحْوُهَا.

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿نَحْنُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا يَقُولُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي حَالِ تَنَاجِيهِمْ بَيْنَهُمْ ﴿إِذْ يَقُولُ أَمْثَلُهُمْ طَرِيقَةً﴾ أَيِ: الْعَاقِلُ الْكَامِلُ فِيهِمْ، ﴿إِنْ لَبِثْتُمْ إِلا يَوْمًا﴾ أَيْ لِقِصَرِ مُدَّةِ الدُّنْيَا فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ [يَوْمَ الْمَعَادِ؛ لِأَنَّ الدُّنْيَا كُلَّها وَإِنْ تَكَرَّرَتْ أَوْقَاتُهَا وَتَعَاقَبَتْ لَيَالِيهَا وَأَيَّامُهَا] وَسَاعَاتُهَا كَأَنَّهَا يَوْمٌ وَاحِدٌ؛ وَلِهَذَا تَسْتَقْصِرُ مُدَّةُ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ: وَكَانَ غَرَضُهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ [دَرْءَ] قِيَامِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِمْ، لِقِصَرِ الْمُدَّةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ يُقْسِمُ الْمُجْرِمُونَ مَا لَبِثُوا غَيْرَ سَاعَةٍ كَذَلِكَ كَانُوا يُؤْفَكُونَ وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعِلْمَ وَالإيمَانَ لَقَدْ لَبِثْتُمْ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْبَعْثِ فَهَذَا يَوْمُ الْبَعْثِ وَلَكِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٥٥، ٥٦] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ نُعَمِّرْكُمْ مَا يَتَذَكَّرُ فِيهِ مَنْ تَذَكَّرَ وَجَاءَكُمُ النَّذِيرُ فَذُوقُوا فَمَا لِلظَّالِمِينَ مِنْ نَصِيرٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ: ٣٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَمْ لَبِثْتُمْ فِي الأرْضِ عَدَدَ سِنِينَ * قَالُوا لَبِثْنَا يَوْمًا أَوْ بَعْضَ يَوْمٍ فَاسْأَلِ الْعَادِّينَ * قَالَ إِنْ لَبِثْتُمْ إِلا قَلِيلا لَوْ أَنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١١٢-١١٤] أَيْ: إِنَّمَا كَانَ لُبثكم فِيهَا قَلِيلًا لَوْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ لَآثَرْتُمُ الْبَاقِيَ عَلَى الْفَانِي، وَلَكِنْ تَصَرَّفْتُمْ فَأَسَأْتُمُ التَّصَرُّفَ، قَدَّمتُم الْحَاضِرَ الْفَانِيَ عَلَى الدَّائِمِ الْبَاقِي.

---

## 20:105-108 — verses 105-108 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And they ask you about the mountains}, meaning: will they remain on the Day of Resurrection or will they vanish? {Say, My Lord will scatter them, a total scattering}, meaning: He will remove them from their places, obliterate them, and make them move away completely.

{And He will leave it}, that is, the earth, {a level, smooth plain}, meaning: a single flat expanse.

Al-qa' is the level part of the earth, and al-safsaf is an emphasis confirming that same meaning. It has also been said that it means that in which there is no vegetation, but the first meaning is preferable, though the second is also intended by necessary implication. This is why He said: {You will not see therein any crookedness or unevenness}, meaning: you will not see on the earth that day any valley or hill, nor any low place or elevated place. This is what Ibn Abbas, Ikrimah, Mujahid, al-Hasan al-Basri, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, and more than one of the salaf have said.

{On that Day they will follow the caller, in whom there is no deviation}, meaning: on the day when they witness these conditions and terrors, they will respond hastening toward the caller, hurrying wherever they are commanded. Had this been in the worldly life it would have been more beneficial for them, but it occurs where it does not benefit them, as the Almighty said: {How well will they hear and how well will they see on the Day they come to Us} [Maryam: 38], and He said: {Racing ahead toward the caller, the disbelievers will say, This is a difficult day} [al-Qamar: 8].

Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi said: God will gather people on the Day of Resurrection in darkness, the sky will be folded up, the stars will scatter, the sun and moon will disappear, and a caller will call out, so the people will follow the sound [and come to him]. That is the meaning of His saying: {On that Day they will follow the caller, in whom there is no deviation}.

Qatadah said: {in whom there is no deviation} means they will not turn away from him.

Abu Salih said: {in whom there is no deviation} means there is no deviation from him.

Regarding His saying: {And voices will be hushed for the Most Merciful}: Ibn Abbas said, they will grow still, and al-Suddi said likewise.

{So you will not hear except a faint sound}: Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, said: it means the tread of footsteps. Ikrimah, Mujahid, al-Dahhak, al-Rabi' ibn Anas, Qatadah, Ibn Zayd and others said the same.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah, from Ibn Abbas, said: {So you will not hear except a faint sound} means a hidden sound. This is also a report from Ikrimah and al-Dahhak.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: {So you will not hear except a faint sound} refers to speech, its whispering, and the tread of footsteps. Sa'id thus combined both interpretations, and this is plausible. As for the tread of footsteps, what is meant is the movement of people toward the place of gathering, which is their walking in stillness and submission. As for hidden speech, it may occur in one state and not in another, for the Almighty said: {On the Day it comes, no soul will speak except by His permission; among them will be the wretched and the blessed} [Hud: 105].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْجِبَالِ﴾ أَيْ: هَلْ تَبْقَى يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ أَوْ تَزُولُ؟ ﴿فَقُلْ يَنْسِفُهَا رَبِّي نَسْفًا﴾ أَيْ: يُذْهِبُهَا عَنْ أَمَاكِنِهَا وَيَمْحَقُهَا وَيُسَيِّرُهَا تَسْيِيرًا.

﴿فَيَذَرُهَا﴾ أَيِ: الْأَرْضَ ﴿قَاعًا صَفْصَفًا﴾ أَيْ: بِسَاطًا وَاحِدًا.

وَالْقَاعُ: هُوَ الْمُسْتَوِي مِنَ الْأَرْضِ. وَالصَّفْصَفُ تَأْكِيدٌ لِمَعْنَى ذَلِكَ، وَقِيلَ: الَّذِي لَا نَبَاتَ فِيهِ. وَالْأَوَّلُ أَوْلَى، وَإِنْ كَانَ الْآخَرُ مُرَادًا أَيْضًا بِاللَّازِمِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا تَرَى فِيهَا عِوَجًا وَلا أَمْتًا﴾ أَيْ: لَا تَرَى فِي الْأَرْضِ يَوْمَئِذٍ وَادِيًا وَلَا رَابِيَةً، وَلَا مَكَانًا مُنْخَفِضًا وَلَا مُرْتَفِعًا، كَذَلِكَ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ.

﴿يَوْمَئِذٍ يَتَّبِعُونَ الدَّاعِيَ لَا عِوَجَ لَهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ يَرَوْنَ هَذِهِ الْأَحْوَالَ وَالْأَهْوَالَ، يَسْتَجِيبُونَ مُسَارِعِينَ إِلَى الدَّاعِي، حَيْثُمَا أُمِرُوا بَادَرُوا إِلَيْهِ، وَلَوْ كَانَ هَذَا فِي الدُّنْيَا لَكَانَ أَنْفَعَ لَهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ حَيْثُ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَسْمِعْ بِهِمْ وَأَبْصِرْ يَوْمَ يَأْتُونَنَا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٣٨] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿مُهْطِعِينَ إِلَى الدَّاعِ يَقُولُ الْكَافِرُونَ هَذَا يَوْمٌ عَسِرٌ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ٨] .

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ القُرَظِي: يَحْشُرُ اللَّهُ النَّاسَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِي ظلمة، وتطوي السماء، وَتَتَنَاثَرُ النُّجُومُ، وَتَذْهَبُ الشَّمْسُ وَالْقَمَرُ، وَيُنَادِي مُنَادٍ، فَيَتْبَعُ النَّاسُ الصَّوْتَ [فَيَأْتُونَهُ] فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَوْمَئِذٍ يَتَّبِعُونَ الدَّاعِيَ لَا عِوَجَ لَهُ﴾ .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿لَا عِوَجَ لَهُ﴾ لَا يَمِيلُونَ عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو صَالِحٍ: ﴿لَا عِوَجَ لَهُ﴾ لَا عِوَجَ عَنْهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَخَشَعَتِ الأصْوَاتُ لِلرَّحْمَنِ﴾ : قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: سَكَنَتْ: وَكَذَا قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ.

﴿فَلا تَسْمَعُ إِلا هَمْسًا﴾ قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي: وَطْءَ الْأَقْدَامِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَالضَّحَاكُ، وَالرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَلا تَسْمَعُ إِلا هَمْسًا﴾ : الصَّوْتُ الْخَفِيُّ. وَهُوَ رِوَايَةٌ عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: ﴿فَلا تَسْمَعُ إِلا هَمْسًا﴾ : الْحَدِيثَ، وَسِرَّهُ، وَوَطْءَ الْأَقْدَامِ. فَقَدْ جَمَعَ سَعِيدٌ كِلَا الْقَوْلَيْنِ وَهُوَ مُحْتَمَلٌ، أَمَّا وَطْءُ الْأَقْدَامِ فَالْمُرَادُ سَعْيُ النَّاسِ إِلَى الْمَحْشَرِ، وَهُوَ مَشْيُهُمْ فِي سُكُونٍ وَخُضُوعٍ. وَأَمَّا الْكَلَامُ الْخَفِيُّ فَقَدْ يَكُونُ فِي حَالٍ دُونَ حَالٍ، فَقَدْ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ يَأْتِ لَا تَكَلَّمُ نَفْسٌ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ فَمِنْهُمْ شَقِيٌّ وَسَعِيدٌ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٠٥] .

---

## 20:109-112 — verses 109-112 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {On that Day} that is, the Day of Resurrection, {intercession will not benefit} that is, before Him, {except him whom the Most Merciful permits, and whose word He approves}, similar to His saying: {Who is it that can intercede with Him except by His permission?} [al-Baqarah: 255], and His saying: {And how many an angel is there in the heavens whose intercession avails nothing, except after Allah gives permission to whom He wills and approves} [al-Najm: 26], and He said: {And they do not intercede except for one whom He has approved} [al-Anbiya: 28], and He said: {And intercession does not benefit with Him except for one whom He permits} [Saba: 23], and He said: {On the Day when the Spirit and the angels stand in ranks, they will not speak except him whom the Most Merciful permits, and he will say what is correct} [al-Naba: 38].

In the two Sahihs, through more than one route, it is related from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who is the master of the children of Adam and the most honored of creation before Allah, Mighty and Majestic, that he said: "I will come beneath the Throne and fall down prostrate before Allah, and He will open for me praises which I cannot enumerate now. He will leave me as long as Allah wills to leave me, then He will say: O Muhammad, raise your head, and speak, you will be heard, and intercede, your intercession will be accepted." He said: "So He will set a limit for me, and I will admit them into Paradise, then I will return." He mentioned this four times, may the prayers and peace of Allah be upon him and upon all the other prophets.

And in the hadith [also], the Almighty says: Bring out of the Fire whoever has in his heart the weight of a grain of faith, and they will bring out a great many creatures. Then He says: Bring out of the Fire whoever has in his heart half the weight of a grain of faith. Bring out of the Fire whoever has in his heart what weighs an atom's weight, whoever has in his heart the least, the least, the least of an atom's weight of faith, the hadith continues.

His saying: {He knows what is before them and what is behind them}, that is, He encompasses in His knowledge all of creation, {while they do not encompass Him in knowledge}, similar to His saying: {And they encompass nothing of His knowledge except what He wills} [al-Baqarah: 255].

His saying: {And faces will be humbled before the Living, the Self-Sustaining}. Ibn Abbas and others said: creation submitted, was humbled and surrendered before its Overpowering Lord, the Living who does not die. Al-Qayyum (the Self-Sustaining) is the One who does not sleep, and He is the Sustainer over everything, managing it and preserving it. He is complete in Himself, the One to whom everything is in need, having no subsistence except through Him.

His saying: {And he has certainly failed who carries injustice}, that is, on the Day of Resurrection, for Allah will render every right to its owner, until He exacts retribution for the hornless sheep from the horned sheep.

In the hadith: "Allah, the Almighty, says: By My might and My majesty, no wrongdoer's injustice will pass beyond Me this Day."

And in the Sahih: "Beware of injustice, for injustice will be layers of darkness on the Day of Resurrection." Utter failure, complete failure, belongs to one who meets Allah while associating partners with Him, for Allah, the Almighty, says: {Indeed, association of partners with Allah is a great injustice} [Luqman: 13].

His saying: {And whoever does righteous deeds while being a believer, he will neither fear injustice nor deprivation}. After mentioning the wrongdoers and the threat against them, He follows with the God-fearing and their ruling, which is that they will not be wronged nor deprived, that is, nothing will be added to their bad deeds and nothing will be diminished from their good deeds. This was said by Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, al-Dahhak, al-Hasan, Qatadah, and others. So injustice (zulm) here means an addition, such that another's sin is placed upon him, and deprivation (hadm) means diminishment.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَئِذٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ﴿لَا تَنْفَعُ الشَّفَاعَةُ﴾ أَيْ: عِنْدَهُ ﴿إِلا مَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ الرَّحْمَنُ وَرَضِيَ لَهُ قَوْلا﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَشْفَعُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٥٥] ،وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَمْ مِنْ مَلَكٍ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ لَا تُغْنِي شَفَاعَتُهُمْ شَيْئًا إِلا مِنْ بَعْدِ أَنْ يَأْذَنَ اللَّهُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَرْضَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٢٦] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلا يَشْفَعُونَ إِلا لِمَنِ ارْتَضَى﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٢٨] وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلا تَنْفَعُ الشَّفَاعَةُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا لِمَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٢٣] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿يَوْمَ يَقُومُ الرُّوحُ وَالْمَلائِكَةُ صَفًّا لَا يَتَكَلَّمُونَ إِلا مَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ الرَّحْمَنُ وَقَالَ صَوَابًا﴾ [النَّبَأِ: ٣٨] .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ سَيِّدُ وَلَدِ آدَمَ، وَأَكْرَمُ الْخَلَائِقِ عَلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "آتِي تَحْتَ الْعَرْشِ، وَأَخِرُّ لِلَّهِ سَاجِدًا، ويَفْتَح عَلَيَّ بِمَحَامِدَ لَا أُحْصِيهَا الْآنَ، فَيَدَعُنِي مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَدَعَنِي، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ارْفَعْ رَأْسَكَ، وَقُلْ يُسْمَعْ وَاشْفَعْ تُشَفَّعْ". قَالَ: "فَيَحِدُّ لِي حَدًّا، فَأُدْخِلُهُمُ الْجَنَّةَ، ثُمَّ أَعُودُ"، فَذَكَرَ أَرْبَعَ مَرَّاتٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عليه وَعَلَى سَائِرِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ.

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ [أَيْضًا] يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: أَخْرِجُوا مِنَ النَّارِ مَنْ كَانَ فِي قَلْبِهِ مِثْقَالُ حَبَّةٍ مِنْ إِيمَانٍ، فَيُخْرِجُون خَلْقًا كَثِيرًا، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: أَخْرِجُوا مِنَ النَّارِ مَنْ كَانَ فِي قَلْبِهِ نِصْفُ مِثْقَالٍ مِنْ إِيمَانٍ، أَخْرِجُوا مِنَ النَّارِ مَنْ كَانَ فِي قَلْبِهِ مَا يَزِنُ ذَرَّةً، مَنْ كَانَ فِي قَلْبِهِ أَدْنَى أَدْنَى أَدْنَى مِثْقَالِ ذَرَّةٍ مِنْ إِيمَانٍ" الْحَدِيثَ. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَعْلَمُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمَا خَلْفَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يُحِيطُ عِلْمًا بِالْخَلَائِقِ كُلِّهِمْ، ﴿وَلا يُحِيطُونَ بِهِ عِلْمًا﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلا يُحِيطُونَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ عِلْمِهِ إِلا بِمَا شَاءَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٥٥] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَعَنَتِ الْوُجُوهُ لِلْحَيِّ الْقَيُّومِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: خَضَعَتْ وَذَلَّتْ وَاسْتَسْلَمَتِ الْخَلَائِقُ لِجَبَّارِهَا الْحَيِّ الَّذِي لَا يَمُوتُ، الْقَيُّومُ: الَّذِي لَا يَنَامُ، وَهُوَ قَيِّمٌ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، يُدَبِّرُهُ وَيَحْفَظُهُ، فَهُوَ الْكَامِلُ فِي نَفْسِهِ، الَّذِي كَلُّ شَيْءٍ فَقِيرٌ إِلَيْهِ، لَا قِوَامَ لَهُ إِلَّا بِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقَدْ خَابَ مَنْ حَمَلَ ظُلْمًا﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ سَيُؤَدِّي كُلَّ حَقٍّ إِلَى صَاحِبِهِ، حَتَّى يَقْتَصَّ لِلشَّاةِ الْجَمَّاءِ مِنَ الشَّاةِ الْقَرْنَاءِ.

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: وَعِزَّتِي وَجَلَالِي، لَا يُجَاوِزُنِي الْيَوْمَ ظُلْمُ ظَالِمٍ" .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ: "إِيَّاكُمْ وَالظُّلْمَ؛ فَإِنَّ الظُّلْمَ ظُلُمَاتٌ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ" . وَالْخَيْبَةُ كُلَّ الْخَيْبَةِ مَنْ لَقِيَ اللَّهَ وَهُوَ مُشْرِكٌ بِهِ؛ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿إِنَّ الشِّرْكَ لَظُلْمٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ١٣]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ يَعْمَلْ مِنَ الصَّالِحَاتِ وَهُوَ مُؤْمِنٌ فَلا يَخَافُ ظُلْمًا وَلا هَضْمًا﴾ لَمَّا ذَكَرَ الظَّالِمِينَ وَوَعِيدَهُمْ، ثَنَّى بِالْمُتَّقِينَ وَحُكْمِهِمْ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُون وَلَا يُهضَمون، أَيْ: لَا يُزَادُ فِي سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ وَلَا يُنْقَصُ مِنْ حَسَنَاتِهِمْ . قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ. فَالظُّلْمُ: الزِّيَادَةُ بِأَنْ يُحْمَلَ عَلَيْهِ ذَنْبُ غَيْرِهِ، وَالْهَضْمُ: النَّقْصُ.

---

## 20:113-114 — verses 113-114 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He says: Since the Day of Return and of recompense for good and evil is bound to occur without doubt, We sent down the Qur'an as a bearer of glad tidings and a warner, in a clear, eloquent Arabic tongue, containing no ambiguity and no incapacity of expression. {And We have explained therein various kinds of warnings, that they might have taqwa (God-consciousness)}, meaning: that they might abandon sins, forbidden acts, and shameful deeds. {Or it might cause them to remember}, meaning: bring about obedience in them and the performance of acts that bring one near to God. {So exalted is Allah, the True King}, meaning: transcendent and holy is the True King, who is Himself true, whose promise is true, whose threat is true, whose messengers are true, whose Paradise is true, whose Fire is true, and everything from Him is true. Part of His justice, Exalted is He, is that He does not punish anyone before warning them and sending messengers and presenting a clear excuse to His creation, so that no one is left with any argument or doubt.

Concerning His saying: {And do not hasten with the Qur'an before its revelation is completed to you}, this is like His saying, Exalted is He, in the surah "I swear by the Day of Resurrection": {Do not move your tongue with it to hasten with it. Indeed, upon Us is its collection and its recitation. So when We have recited it, follow its recitation. Then upon Us is its explanation} [al-Qiyamah: 16-19]. It is established in the Sahih, from Ibn Abbas, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to struggle intensely with the revelation, and among the things he would do was move his tongue along with it. So Allah sent down this verse. This means that he, peace be upon him, whenever Jibril came to him with the revelation, every time Jibril spoke a verse he would say it along with him, out of his intense eagerness to memorize the Qur'an. So Allah, Exalted is He, guided him to what was easier and lighter for him, so that it would not be a hardship upon him. He said: {Do not move your tongue with it to hasten with it. Indeed, upon Us is its collection and its recitation}, meaning: that We will gather it in your breast, and then you will recite it to the people without forgetting anything of it. {So when We have recited it, follow its recitation. Then upon Us is its explanation}. And He said in this verse: {And do not hasten with the Qur'an before its revelation is completed to you}, meaning: rather, be silent, and when the angel finishes reciting it to you, then recite it after him. {And say: My Lord, increase me in knowledge}, meaning: increase me in knowledge from Yourself.

Ibn Uyaynah, may Allah have mercy on him, said: He ﷺ continued to increase [in knowledge] until Allah, Mighty and Majestic is He, took his soul.

For this reason it has come in the hadith: "Indeed Allah made the revelation follow continuously upon His Messenger, until the revelation was at its greatest on the day the Messenger of Allah ﷺ passed away." Ibn Majah said: [chain] Abu Hurairah, may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to say: "O Allah, benefit me by what You have taught me, and teach me what benefits me, and increase me in knowledge, and praise be to Allah in every circumstance."

Al-Tirmidhi transmitted it from Abu Kurayb, from Abdullah ibn Numayr, with the same chain, and said: gharib (singular) from this route. Al-Bazzar narrated it from Amr ibn Ali al-Fallas, from Abu Asim, from Musa ibn Ubaydah, with the same chain, and added at the end: "And I seek refuge in Allah from the state of the people of the Fire."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ: وَلَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْمَعَادِ وَالْجَزَاءِ بِالْخَيْرِ وَالشَّرِّ وَاقِعًا لَا مَحَالَةَ، أَنْزَلْنَا الْقُرْآنَ بَشِيرًا وَنَذِيرًا، بِلِسَانٍ عَرَبِيٍّ مُبِينٍ فَصِيحٍ لَا لَبْسَ فِيهِ وَلَا عِيَّ، ﴿وَصَرَّفْنَا فِيهِ مِنَ الْوَعِيدِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَّقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَتْرُكُونَ الْمَآثِمَ وَالْمَحَارِمَ وَالْفَوَاحِشَ، ﴿أَوْ يُحْدِثُ لَهُمْ ذِكْرًا﴾ وَهُوَ إِيجَادُ الطَّاعَةِ وَفِعْلُ الْقُرُبَاتِ. ﴿فَتَعَالَى اللَّهُ الْمَلِكُ الْحَقُّ﴾ أَيْ: تَنَزَّهَ وَتَقَدَّسَ الْمَلِكُ الْحَقُّ، الَّذِي هُوَ حَقٌّ، وَوَعْدُهُ حَقٌّ، وَوَعِيدُهُ حَقٌّ، وَرُسُلُهُ حَقٌّ، وَالْجَنَّةُ حَقٌّ، وَالنَّارُ حَقٌّ، وَكُلُّ شَيْءٍ مِنْهُ حَقٌّ. وَعَدْلُهُ تَعَالَى أَلَّا يُعَذِّبَ أَحَدًا قَبْلَ الْإِنْذَارِ وَبَعْثَةِ الرُّسُلِ وَالْإِعْذَارِ إِلَى خَلْقِهِ؛ لِئَلَّا يَبْقَى لِأَحَدٍ حُجَّةٌ وَلَا شُبْهَةٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تَعْجَلْ بِالْقُرْآنِ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ يُقْضَى إِلَيْكَ وَحْيُهُ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى فِي سُورَةِ "لَا أُقْسِمُ بِيَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ" ﴿لَا تُحَرِّكْ بِهِ لِسَانَكَ لِتَعْجَلَ بِهِ * إِنَّ عَلَيْنَا جَمْعَهُ وَقُرْآنَهُ * فَإِذَا قَرَأْنَاهُ فَاتَّبِعْ قُرْآنَهُ ثُمَّ إِنَّ عَلَيْنَا بَيَانَهُ﴾ [الْقِيَامَةِ: ١٦-١٩] ، وَثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يُعَالِجُ مِنَ الْوَحْيِ شِدَّةً، فَكَانَ مِمَّا يُحَرِّكُ لِسَانَهُ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ يَعْنِي: أَنَّهُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، كَانَ إِذَا جَاءَهُ جِبْرِيلُ بِالْوَحْيِ، كُلَّمَا قَالَ جِبْرِيلُ آيَةً قَالَهَا مَعَهُ، مِنْ شِدَّةِ حِرْصِهِ عَلَى حِفْظِ الْقُرْآنِ، فَأَرْشَدَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى إِلَى مَا هُوَ الْأَسْهَلُ وَالْأَخَفُّ فِي حَقِّهِ؛ لِئَلَّا يَشُقَّ عَلَيْهِ. فَقَالَ: ﴿لَا تُحَرِّكْ بِهِ لِسَانَكَ لِتَعْجَلَ بِهِ * إِنَّ عَلَيْنَا جَمْعَهُ وَقُرْآنَهُ﴾ أَيْ: أَنْ نَجْمَعَهُ فِي صَدْرِكَ، ثُمَّ تَقْرَأَهُ عَلَى النَّاسِ مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنْ تَنْسَى مِنْهُ شَيْئًا، ﴿فَإِذَا قَرَأْنَاهُ فَاتَّبِعْ قُرْآنَهُ * ثُمَّ إِنَّ عَلَيْنَا بَيَانَهُ﴾ وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَلا تَعْجَلْ بِالْقُرْآنِ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ يُقْضَى إِلَيْكَ وَحْيُهُ﴾ أَيْ: بَلْ أَنْصِتْ، فَإِذَا فَرَغَ الْمَلَكُ مِنْ قِرَاءَتِهِ عَلَيْكَ فَاقْرَأْهُ بَعْدَهُ، ﴿وَقُلْ رَبِّ زِدْنِي عِلْمًا﴾ أَيْ: زِدْنِي مِنْكَ عِلْمًا.

قَالَ ابْنُ عُيَيْنَة، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: وَلَمْ يَزَلْ ﷺ فِي زِيَادَةٍ [مِنَ الْعِلْمِ] حَتَّى تَوَفَّاهُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَابَعَ الْوَحْيَ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ، حَتَّى كَانَ الْوَحْيُ أَكْثَرَ مَا كَانَ يَوْمَ تُوُفِّيَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، حدثنا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ نُمَيْر، عَنْ مُوسَى بْنِ عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "اللَّهُمَّ انْفَعْنِي بِمَا علَّمتني، وَعَلِّمْنِي مَا يَنْفَعُنِي، وَزِدْنِي عِلْمًا، وَالْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ عَلَى كُلِّ حَالٍ" .

وَأَخْرَجَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، عَنِ أَبِي كُرَيْب، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ نُمَيْر، بِهِ. وَقَالَ: غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ. وَرَوَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَلِيٍّ الْفَلَّاسِ، عَنِ أَبِي عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ مُوسَى بْنِ عُبَيْدَةَ، بِهِ. وَزَادَ فِي آخِرِهِ: "وَأَعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ من حال أهل النار".

---

## 20:115-122 — verses 115-122 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Ahmad ibn Sinan told us, Asbat ibn Muhammad told us, al-A'mash told us, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: Man (al-insan) was only named thus because a covenant was made with him and he forgot (nasiya). And 'Ali ibn Abi Talha likewise narrated this from him.

Mujahid and al-Hasan said: it means "he abandoned."

His saying, {And when We said to the angels, prostrate to Adam}: The Exalted mentions here the honoring and ennobling of Adam, and how He preferred him with a preference over many of those He created.

The discussion of this story has already preceded in Surat al-Baqarah, and in al-A'raf, and in al-Hijr and al-Kahf, and it will come again at the end of Surat Sad, if Allah the Exalted wills. He mentions therein the creation of Adam and His command to the angels to prostrate to him as an honor and ennoblement, and He makes clear the ancient enmity of Iblis toward the children of Adam and toward their father before them. For this reason the Exalted said: {So they prostrated, except Iblis; he refused}, meaning he abstained and was arrogant. {Then We said, O Adam, indeed this is an enemy to you and to your wife}, meaning Eve (peace be upon them both), {so let him not expel you both from the Garden, so that you would suffer}, meaning: beware lest he strive to expel you from it, so that you would toil, be worn out, and suffer in seeking your provision, whereas here you are in a pleasant and comfortable life, with no burden and no hardship.

{Indeed it is for you that you will not hunger therein nor be unclothed}: He paired hunger and nakedness together because hunger is the humiliation of the inward, and nakedness is the humiliation of the outward.

{And that you will not thirst therein nor be exposed to the sun}: These two are likewise paired opposites. Thirst is the heat of the inward, namely thirst itself, and exposure to the sun's heat (duha) is the heat of the outward.

His saying: {Then Satan whispered to him, saying, O Adam, shall I direct you to the tree of eternity and a kingdom that does not decay?}. It has already preceded that he {lowered them both by deception} [al-A'raf: 22], and {he swore to them both, indeed I am to you both among the sincere advisors} [al-A'raf: 21]. It has also already preceded that Allah the Exalted revealed to Adam and his wife that they should eat from every fruit, but not approach this particular tree in the Garden. Iblis did not cease his efforts with them both until they ate from it. And it was the tree of eternity, meaning the tree such that whoever eats from it would live forever and remain permanently. Mention of the tree of eternity has come in hadith. Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said: Shu'bah told us, from Abu al-Dahhak, I heard Abu Hurayrah narrating, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Indeed in the Garden there is a tree in whose shade a rider would travel for a hundred years without crossing it, and it is the tree of eternity." Imam Ahmad also narrated it.

His saying: {So they both ate from it, and their private parts became exposed to them}. Ibn Abi Hatim said:

[chain] Ubayy ibn Ka'b said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed Allah created Adam as a tall man with abundant hair on his head, like a towering palm tree. When he tasted the tree, his garment fell away from him, and the first thing that appeared of him was his private part. When he looked at his private part he began to run about in the Garden, and a tree caught hold of his hair, and he struggled with it. Then the Most Merciful called out: O Adam, are you fleeing from Me? When he heard the speech of the Most Merciful he said: O my Lord, no, but out of shame. Tell me, if I repent and return, will I be brought back to the Garden? He said: Yes." That is the meaning of His saying: {Then Adam received from his Lord words, and He turned to him in mercy}.

This chain is disconnected between al-Hasan and Ubayy ibn Ka'b, for he did not hear it from him, and there is also doubt regarding its being raised to the Prophet ﷺ.

His saying: {And they both began to fasten together upon themselves from the leaves of the Garden}. Mujahid said: they patched leaves together in the manner of a garment. Qatadah and al-Suddi said likewise.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said, regarding {And they both began to fasten together upon themselves from the leaves of the Garden}: He said, they pulled off fig leaves and placed them over their private parts.

His saying: {And Adam disobeyed his Lord and erred. Then his Lord chose him, and turned to him in mercy, and guided him}. Al-Bukhari said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, said: "Musa argued with Adam, and said to him: Are you the one who brought people out of the Garden through your sin and caused them to suffer? Adam said: O Musa, you are the one whom Allah chose for His messages and for His speech to you directly. Do you blame me for a matter that Allah had already written upon me before He created me, or: that Allah had already decreed upon me before He created me?" The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "So Adam prevailed over Musa in argument." This hadith has multiple chains in the two Sahihs and other collections of musnads.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] I heard Abu Hurayrah say: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Adam and Musa argued before their Lord, and Adam prevailed over Musa in argument. Musa said: Are you the one whom Allah created with His hand, and breathed into you from His spirit, and made His angels prostrate to you, and settled you in His Garden, then you caused people to be brought down to earth through your error? Adam said: You are Musa, whom Allah chose for His message and His speech, and gave you the Tablets in which is an explanation of everything, and brought you near in intimate discourse. So how long before I was created did you find that Allah had written the Torah? Musa said: Forty years. Adam said: Then did you find in it {And Adam disobeyed his Lord and erred}? He said: Yes. Adam said: Then do you blame me for having done a deed that Allah had written upon me to do, forty years before He created me?" The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "So Adam prevailed over Musa in argument."

Al-Harith said: And Abd al-Rahman ibn Hurmuz also related this to me, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَان، حَدَّثَنَا أَسْبَاطُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ الْإِنْسَانَ لِأَنَّهُ عَهِدَ إِلَيْهِ فَنَسِيَ. وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَالْحَسَنُ: تَرَكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِذْ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلائِكَةِ اسْجُدُوا لآدَمَ﴾ يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى تَشْرِيفَ آدَمَ وَتَكْرِيمَهُ، وَمَا فَضَّلَهُ بِهِ عَلَى كَثِيرٍ مِمَّنْ خَلَقَ تَفْضِيلًا.

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةِ فِي سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ" وَفِي "الْأَعْرَافِ" وَفِي "الْحِجْرِ" وَ"الْكَهْفِ" وَسَيَأْتِي فِي آخِرِ سُورَةِ "ص" [إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى] . يَذْكُرُ فِيهَا تَعَالَى خَلْقَ آدَمَ وأَمْرَه الْمَلَائِكَةَ بِالسُّجُودِ لَهُ تَشْرِيفًا وَتَكْرِيمًا، وَيُبَيِّنُ عَدَاوَةَ إِبْلِيسَ لِبَنِي آدَمَ وَلِأَبِيهِمْ قَدِيمًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَسَجَدُوا إِلا إِبْلِيسَ أَبَى﴾ أَيِ: امْتَنَعَ وَاسْتَكْبَرَ. ﴿فَقُلْنَا يَا آدَمُ إِنَّ هَذَا عَدُوٌّ لَكَ وَلِزَوْجِكَ﴾ يَعْنِي: حَوَّاءَ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ ﴿فَلا يُخْرِجَنَّكُمَا مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ فَتَشْقَى﴾ أَيْ: إِيَّاكَ أَنْ يَسْعَى فِي إِخْرَاجِكَ مِنْهَا، فَتَتْعَبَ وَتُعَنَّى وَتَشْقَى فِي طَلَبِ رِزْقِكَ، فَإِنَّكَ هَاهُنَا فِي عَيْشٍ رَغِيدٍ هَنِيءٍ، لَا كُلْفَةَ وَلَا مَشَقَّةَ.

﴿إِنَّ لَكَ أَلا تَجُوعَ فِيهَا وَلا تَعْرَى﴾ إِنَّمَا قَرَنَ بَيْنَ الْجُوعِ والعُرْي؛ لِأَنَّ الْجُوعَ ذُلّ الْبَاطِنِ، وَالْعُرْيَ ذُلّ الظَّاهِرِ.

﴿وَأَنَّكَ لَا تَظْمَأُ فِيهَا وَلا تَضْحَى﴾ وَهَذَانَ أَيْضًا مُتَقَابِلَانِ، فَالظَّمَأُ: حَرُّ الْبَاطِنِ، وَهُوَ الْعَطَشُ. وَالضُّحَى: حَرُّ الظَّاهِرِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَوَسْوَسَ إِلَيْهِ الشَّيْطَانُ قَالَ يَا آدَمُ هَلْ أَدُلُّكَ عَلَى شَجَرَةِ الْخُلْدِ وَمُلْكٍ لَا يَبْلَى﴾ قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ أَنَّهُ ﴿دَلاهُمَا بِغُرُور﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٢٢] ؛ ﴿وَقَاسَمَهُمَا إِنِّي لَكُمَا لَمِنَ النَّاصِحِينَ﴾ [الأعراف: ٢١] . وقد تَقَدَّمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى أَوْحَى إِلَى آدَمَ وَزَوْجَتِهِ أَنَّ يَأْكُلَا مِنْ كُلِّ الثِّمَارِ، وَلَا يَقْرَبَا هَذِهِ الشَّجَرَةَ الْمُعَيَّنَةَ فِي الْجَنَّةِ. فَلَمْ يَزَلْ بِهِمَا إِبْلِيسُ حَتَّى أَكَلَا مِنْهَا، وَكَانَتْ شجرةَ الْخُلْدِ -يَعْنِي: الَّتِي مَنْ أَكَلَ مِنْهَا خُلِّدَ وَدَامَ مُكْثُهُ. وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ ذِكْرُ شَجَرَةِ الْخُلْدِ، فَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ عَنْ أَبِي الضَّحَّاكِ سَمِعْتُ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ يُحَدِّثُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ فِي الْجَنَّةِ شَجَرَةً يَسِيرُ الرَّاكِبُ فِي ظِلِّهَا مِائَةَ عَامٍ، مَا يَقْطَعُهَا وَهِيَ شَجَرَةُ الْخُلْدِ". وَرَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ. .

وَقَوْلُ: ﴿فَأَكَلا مِنْهَا فَبَدَتْ لَهُمَا سَوْآتُهُمَا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ بْنِ إِشْكَابَ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي عَرُوبة، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ آدَمَ رَجُلًا طِوَالًا كَثِيرَ شَعْرِ الرَّأْسِ، كَأَنَّهُ نَخْلَةٌ سَحُوق. فَلَمَّا ذَاقَ الشَّجَرَةَ سَقَطَ عَنْهُ لِبَاسُهُ، فَأَوَّلُ مَا بَدَا مِنْهُ عَوْرَتُهُ. فَلَمَّا نَظَرَ إِلَى عَوْرَتِهِ جَعَلَ يَشْتَد فِي الْجَنَّةِ، فأخذتْ شعرَه شَجَرَةٌ، فَنَازَعَهَا، فَنَادَى الرَّحْمَنُ: يَا آدَمُ، منِّي تَفِرُّ؟ فَلَمَّا سَمِعَ كَلَامَ الرَّحْمَنِ قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، لَا وَلَكِنِ اسْتِحْيَاءً أَرَأَيْتَ إِنْ تُبْتُ وَرَجَعْتُ، أَعَائِدِي إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ" فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَتَلَقَّى آدَمُ مِنْ رَبِّهِ كَلِمَاتٍ فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ﴾ 

وَهَذَا مُنْقَطِعٌ بَيْنَ الْحَسَنِ وأُبيّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ، فَلَمْ يَسْمَعْهُ مِنْهُ، وَفِي رَفْعِهِ نَظَرٌ أَيْضًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَطَفِقَا يَخْصِفَانِ عَلَيْهِمَا مِنْ وَرَقِ الْجَنَّةِ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يُرَقِّعَانِ كَهَيْئَةِ الثَّوْبِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرٌ، عَنْ عَوْنٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي لَيْلَى، عَنْ المِنْهال، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَطَفِقَا يَخْصِفَانِ عَلَيْهِمَا مِنْ وَرَقِ الْجَنَّةِ﴾ قَالَ: يَنْزِعَانِ وَرَقَ التِّينِ، فَيَجْعَلَانِهِ عَلَى سَوْآتِهِمَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَعَصَى آدَمُ رَبَّهُ فَغَوَى ثُمَّ اجْتَبَاهُ رَبُّهُ فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ وَهَدَى﴾ قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا قُتَيْبَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَيُّوبُ بْنُ النَّجَّارِ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ أَبِي كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "حَاجَّ مُوسَى آدَمَ، فَقَالَ لَهُ: أَنْتَ الَّذِي أَخْرَجْتَ النَّاسَ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ بِذَنْبِكَ وَأَشْقَيْتَهُمْ؟ قَالَ آدَمُ: يَا مُوسَى، أَنْتَ الَّذِي اصْطَفَاكَ اللَّهُ بِرِسَالَاتِهِ وَبِكَلَامِهِ، أَتَلُومُنِي عَلَى أَمْرٍ قَدْ كَتَبَهُ اللَّهُ عَلَيَّ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَخْلُقَنِي -أَوْ: قَدَّرَهُ اللَّهُ عَلَيَّ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَخْلُقَنِي -" قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "فحج آدم موسى". وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ لَهُ طُرُقٌ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، وَغَيْرِهِمَا مِنَ الْمَسَانِيدِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ وهب، أَخْبَرَنِي أَنَسُ بْنُ عِيَاضٍ، عَنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ أَبِي ذُبَابَ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هُرْمُزَ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ يَقُولُ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "حَجَّ آدمُ وَمُوسَى عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمَا، فَحَجَّ آدَمُ مُوسَى، قَالَ مُوسَى: أَنْتَ الَّذِي خَلَقَكَ اللَّهُ بِيَدِهِ، وَنَفَخَ فِيكَ مِنْ رُوحِهِ، وَأَسْجَدَ لَكَ مَلَائِكَتَهُ، وَأَسْكَنَكَ فِي جَنَّتِهِ، ثُمَّ أَهْبَطْتَ النَّاسَ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ بِخَطِيئَتِكَ؟ قَالَ آدَمُ: أَنْتَ مُوسَى الَّذِي اصْطَفَاكَ اللَّهُ بِرِسَالَتِهِ وَكَلَامِهِ، وَأَعْطَاكَ الْأَلْوَاحَ فِيهَا تِبْيَانُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، وَقَرَّبَكَ نَجِيًّا، فَبِكَمْ وجدتَ اللَّهَ كَتَبَ التَّوْرَاةَ [قَبْلَ أَنْ أُخْلَقَ] قَالَ مُوسَى: بِأَرْبَعِينَ عَامًا. قَالَ آدَمُ: فَهَلْ وجدتَ فِيهَا ﴿وَعَصَى آدَمُ رَبَّهُ فَغَوَى﴾ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: أَفَتَلُومُنِي عَلَى أَنْ عملتُ عَمَلًا كَتَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيَّ أَنْ أَعْمَلَهُ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَخْلُقَنِي بِأَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً". قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "فَحَجَّ آدَمُ مُوسَى".

قَالَ الْحَارِثُ: وَحَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ هُرْمزُ بِذَلِكَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ. .

---

## 20:123-126 — verses 123-126 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says to Adam, Eve, and Iblis: {Descend from it, all of you}, meaning: all of you from Paradise. We have already elaborated on this in Surat al-Baqarah.

{Some of you being enemies to others}: he said: Adam and his offspring, and Iblis and his offspring.

His statement: {And if there comes to you guidance from Me}, Abu al-Aliyah said: the prophets and messengers and clarification.

{Then whoever follows My guidance will not go astray nor suffer}: Ibn Abbas said: will not go astray in this world, nor suffer in the Hereafter.

{And whoever turns away from My remembrance}, meaning: opposes My command and what I have sent down upon My messenger, turns away from it, forgets it deliberately, and takes his guidance from other than it, {then indeed for him is a straitened life}, meaning: in this world. He has no tranquility and no expansion of his chest, rather his chest is tight and constricted because of his misguidance, even if his outward state is one of ease, and he wears what he wishes, eats what he wishes, and dwells wherever he wishes. For as long as his heart has not attained certainty and guidance, he remains in anxiety, confusion, and doubt, forever wavering in uncertainty. This is part of the straitened life.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas: {then indeed for him is a straitened life}, he said: this is wretchedness.

Al-Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas: {then indeed for him is a straitened life}, he said: any wealth I give to a servant of Mine, whether little or much, if he does not have fear of Me regarding it, there is no good in it, and that is the straitened life. It is also said: certain misguided people turned away from the truth while living in worldly abundance, arrogant, and yet their life was straitened. That was because they believed that God would not withhold their provision from them, due to their evil assumption about God and their denial. So when a servant denies God, has an evil assumption of Him, and lacks trust in Him, his life becomes hard upon him, and that is the straitening.

Al-Dahhak said: it is evil deeds and impure sustenance. Ikrimah and Malik ibn Dinar said likewise.

Sufyan ibn Uyaynah reported from Abu Hazim, from Abu Salamah, from Abu Said, regarding His statement {a straitened life}: he said: his grave will be constricted upon him until his ribs interlock within it. Abu Hatim al-Razi said: al-Numan ibn Abi Ayyash is known by the kunyah Abu Salamah.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Zurah told us, Safwan told us, al-Walid told us, Abdullah ibn Lahiah told us, from Darraj, from Abu al-Haytham, from Abu Said, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said regarding the statement of God, Mighty and Majestic, {then indeed for him is a straitened life}: "The squeezing of the grave." The mawquf (halted report) version is more authentic.

Ibn Abi Hatim also said: [chain] al-Rabi ibn Sulayman told us, Asad ibn Musa told us, Ibn Lahiah told us, Darraj Abu al-Samh told us, from Ibn Hujayrah, whose name was Abd al-Rahman, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, who said: "The believer in his grave is in a green meadow, his grave is widened for him to seventy cubits, and his grave is illuminated for him like the moon on the night of the full moon. Do you know regarding what this verse was revealed: {then indeed for him is a straitened life}? Do you know what the straitened life is?" They said: God and His Messenger know best. He said: "It is the punishment of the disbeliever in his grave. By the One in whose hand is my soul, ninety-nine dragons are given power over him. Do you know what a dragon is? Ninety-nine serpents, each serpent having seven heads, which blow into his body, sting him, and lacerate him until the Day they are resurrected."

Raising this to the Prophet ﷺ as a marfu (elevated) report is extremely rejected (munkar).

Al-Bazzar said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Yahya al-Azdi told us, Muhammad ibn Amr told us, Hisham ibn Sad told us, from Said ibn Abi Hilal, from Abu Hujayrah, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ regarding the statement of God, Mighty and Majestic, {then indeed for him is a straitened life}, he said: "The straitened life which God the Almighty spoke of is that ninety-nine serpents are given power over him, gnawing at his flesh until the Hour is established."

He also said: [chain] Abu Zurah told us, Abu al-Walid told us, Hammad ibn Salamah told us, from Muhammad ibn Amr, from Abu Salamah, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ regarding {then indeed for him is a straitened life}, he said: "The punishment of the grave." A good (jayyid) chain.

His statement: {And We will gather him on the Day of Resurrection blind}: Mujahid, Abu Salih, and al-Suddi said: he will have no argument.

Ikrimah said: everything will be made blind to him except Hellfire.

It is also possible that the meaning is: he will be gathered or resurrected to the Fire blind in both physical sight and insight, as the Almighty said: {And We will gather them on the Day of Resurrection, on their faces, blind, dumb, and deaf. Their refuge is Hell; every time it subsides, We increase them in blazing fire} [al-Isra: 97]. That is why he says: {My Lord, why have You gathered me blind while I was truly able to see?}, meaning: in this world.

{He will say: Thus it is. Our signs came to you and you forgot them, and thus this Day you will be forgotten}, meaning: since you turned away from the signs of God and treated them as one who does not remember them, after they had reached you, deliberately forgetting them, turning away from them, and neglecting them, so too We will treat you today as one who forgets you, {so today We will forget them just as they forgot the meeting of this Day of theirs} [al-Araf: 51]. For the recompense is of the same kind as the deed. As for forgetting the wording of the Qur'an while understanding its meaning and acting according to its requirements, this is not included in this specific threat, even though it is threatened from another angle, for the Sunnah has come with a firm prohibition and severe threat concerning that. Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Khalaf ibn al-Walid told us, Khalid told us, from Yazid ibn Abi Ziyad, from Isa ibn Faid, from a man, from Sad ibn Ubadah, may God be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There is no man who reads the Qur'an and then forgets it, except that he will meet God on the Day he meets Him afflicted with leprosy."

Then Imam Ahmad related it through the hadith of Yazid ibn Abi Ziyad, from Isa ibn Faid, from Ubadah ibn al-Samit, from the Prophet ﷺ, mentioning the same thing exactly.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِآدَمَ وَحَوَّاءَ وَإِبْلِيسَ: اهْبِطُوا مِنْهَا جَمِيعًا، أَيْ: مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ كُلُّكُمْ. وَقَدْ بَسَطْنَا ذَلِكَ فِي سُورَةِ الْبَقَرَةِ".

﴿بَعْضُكُمْ لِبَعْضٍ عَدُوٌّ﴾ قَالَ: آدَمُ وَذُرِّيَّتُهُ، وَإِبْلِيسُ وَذُرِّيَّتُهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَإِمَّا يَأْتِيَنَّكُمْ مِنِّي هُدًى﴾ قَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ: الْأَنْبِيَاءُ وَالرُّسُلُ وَالْبَيَانُ.

﴿فَمَنِ اتَّبَعَ هُدَايَ فَلا يَضِلُّ وَلا يَشْقَى﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: لَا يَضِلُّ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَلَا يَشْقَى فِي الْآخِرَةِ.

﴿وَمَنْ أَعْرَضَ عَنْ ذِكْرِي﴾ أَيْ: خَالَفَ أَمْرِي، وَمَا أَنْزَلْتُهُ عَلَى رَسُولِي، أَعْرَضَ عَنْهُ وَتَنَاسَاهُ وَأَخَذَ مِنْ غَيْرِهِ هُدَاهُ ﴿فَإِنَّ لَهُ مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَلَا طُمَأْنِينَةَ لَهُ، وَلَا انْشِرَاحَ لِصَدْرِهِ، بَلْ صَدْرُهُ [ضَيِّقٌ] حَرَج لِضَلَالِهِ، وَإِنْ تَنَعَّم ظَاهِرُهُ، وَلَبِسَ مَا شَاءَ وَأَكَلَ مَا شَاءَ، وَسَكَنَ حَيْثُ شَاءَ، فَإِنَّ قلبه مَا لَمْ يَخْلُصْ إِلَى الْيَقِينِ وَالْهُدَى، فَهُوَ فِي قَلَقٍ وَحَيْرَةٍ وَشَكٍّ، فَلَا يَزَالُ فِي رِيبَةٍ يَتَرَدَّدُ. فَهَذَا مِنْ ضَنْكِ الْمَعِيشَةِ.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَإِنَّ لَهُ مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ قَالَ: الشَّقَاءُ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَإِنَّ لَهُ مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ قَالَ: كُلُّ مَالٍ أَعْطَيْتُهُ عَبْدًا مِنْ عِبَادِي، قَلَّ أَوْ كَثُرَ، لَا يَتَّقِينِي فِيهِ، فَلَا خَيْرَ فِيهِ، وَهُوَ الضَّنْكُ فِي الْمَعِيشَةِ. وَيُقَالُ: إِنْ قَوْمًا ضُلالا أَعْرَضُوا عَنِ الْحَقِّ، وَكَانُوا فِي سَعَةٍ مِنَ الدُّنْيَا مُتَكَبِّرِينَ، فَكَانَتْ مَعِيشَتُهُمْ ضَنْكًا؛ [وَ] ذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَرَوْنَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ لَيْسَ مُخَلِّفًا لَهُمْ مَعَايِشَهُمْ، مِنْ سُوءِ ظَنِّهِمْ بِاللَّهِ وَالتَّكْذِيبِ، فَإِذَا كَانَ الْعَبْدُ يُكَذِّبُ بِاللَّهِ، وَيُسِيءُ الظَّنَّ بِهِ وَالثِّقَةَ بِهِ اشْتَدَّتْ عَلَيْهِ مَعِيشَتُهُ، فَذَلِكَ الضَّنْكُ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: هُوَ الْعَمَلُ السَّيِّئُ، وَالرِّزْقُ الْخَبِيثُ، وَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَمَالِكُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنِ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ قَالَ: يُضَيَّقُ عَلَيْهِ قَبْرُهُ، حَتَّى تَخْتَلِفَ أَضْلَاعُهُ فِيهِ. قَالَ أَبُو حَاتِمٍ الرَّازِيُّ: النُّعْمَانُ بْنُ أَبِي عَيَّاشٍ يُكَنَّى أَبَا سَلَمَةَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُرْعة، حَدَّثَنَا صَفْوَانُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بن لَهِيعَةَ، عَنْ دَرَّاج، عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿فَإِنَّ لَهُ مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ قَالَ: "ضَمَّةُ الْقَبْرِ" الْمَوْقُوفُ أَصَحُّ. 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ سُلَيْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَسَدُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا دَرَّاجٌ أَبُو السَّمْحِ، عَنِ ابْنِ حُجَيْرة -اسْمُهُ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ -عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: الْمُؤْمِنُ فِي قَبْرِهِ فِي رَوْضَةٍ خَضْرَاءَ، وَيُرَحَّبُ لَهُ فِي قَبْرِهِ سَبْعُونَ ذِرَاعًا، وَيُنَوَّرُ لَهُ قَبْرُهُ كَالْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ الْبَدْرِ، أَتَدْرُونَ فِيمَ أُنْزِلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿فَإِنَّ لَهُ مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ ؟ أَتَدْرُونَ مَا الْمَعِيشَةُ الضَّنْكُ؟ " قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: عَذَابُ الْكَافِرِ فِي قَبْرِهِ، وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّهُ لَيُسَلَّطُ عَلَيْهِ تِسْعَةٌ وَتِسْعُونَ تِنِّينًا، أَتَدْرُونَ مَا التِّنِّينُ؟ تِسْعَةٌ وَتِسْعُونَ حَيَّةً، لِكُلِّ حَيَّةٍ سَبْعَةُ رُؤُوسٍ، يَنْفُخُونَ فِي جِسْمِهِ، وَيَلْسَعُونَهُ وَيَخْدِشُونَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ يُبْعَثُونَ". .

رَفْعُهُ مُنْكَرٌ جِدًّا.

وَقَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يَحْيَى الْأَزْدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي هِلَالٍ، [عَنْ أَبِي حُجَيْرة] عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿فَإِنَّ لَهُ مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ قَالَ: "الْمَعِيشَةُ الضَّنْكُ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: أَنَّهُ يُسَلَّطُ عَلَيْهِ تسعة وتسعون حَيَّةً، يَنْهَشُونَ لَحْمَهُ حَتَّى تَقُومَ السَّاعَةُ" .

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُرْعَة، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: ﴿فَإِنَّ لَهُ مَعِيشَةً ضَنْكًا﴾ قَالَ: "عَذَابُ الْقَبْرِ". إِسْنَادٌ جَيِّدٌ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنَحْشُرُهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ أَعْمَى﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: لَا حُجَّةَ لَهُ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: عُمِّي عَلَيْهِ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ إِلَّا جَهَنَّمَ.

وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمُرَادُ: أَنَّهُ يُحشَر أَوْ يُبْعَثُ إِلَى النَّارِ أَعْمَى الْبَصَرِ وَالْبَصِيرَةِ أَيْضًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنَحْشُرُهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ عُمْيًا وَبُكْمًا وَصُمًّا مَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ كُلَّمَا خَبَتْ زِدْنَاهُمْ سَعِيرًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٩٧] . وَلِهَذَا يَقُولُ: ﴿رَبِّ لِمَ حَشَرْتَنِي أَعْمَى وَقَدْ كُنْتُ بَصِيرًا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا.

﴿قَالَ كَذَلِكَ أَتَتْكَ آيَاتُنَا فَنَسِيتَهَا وَكَذَلِكَ الْيَوْمَ تُنْسَى﴾ أَيْ: لَمَّا أَعْرَضْتَ عَنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ، وعامَلْتها مُعَامَلَةَ مَنْ لَمْ يَذْكُرْهَا، بَعْدَ بَلَاغِهَا إِلَيْكَ تَنَاسَيْتَهَا وَأَعْرَضْتَ عَنْهَا وَأَغْفَلْتَهَا، كَذَلِكَ نُعَامِلُكَ [الْيَوْمَ] مُعَامَلَةَ مَنْ يَنْسَاكَ ﴿فَالْيَوْمَ نَنْسَاهُمْ كَمَا نَسُوا لِقَاءَ يَوْمِهِمْ هَذَا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٥١] فَإِنَّ الْجَزَاءَ مِنْ جِنْسِ الْعَمَلِ، فَأَمَّا نِسْيَانُ لَفْظِ الْقُرْآنِ مَعَ فَهْمِ مَعْنَاهُ وَالْقِيَامِ بِمُقْتَضَاهُ، فَلَيْسَ دَاخِلًا فِي هَذَا الْوَعِيدِ الْخَاصِّ، وَإِنْ كَانَ مُتَوَعدًا عَلَيْهِ مِنْ جِهَةٍ أُخْرَى، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ وَرَدَتِ السُّنَّةُ بِالنَّهْيِ الْأَكِيدِ، وَالْوَعِيدِ الشَّدِيدِ فِي ذَلِكَ، قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا خَلَفُ بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدٌ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي زِيَادٍ، عَنْ عِيسَى بْنِ فَائِدٍ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنْ سَعْدِ بْنِ عُبَادَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْ رَجُلٍ قَرَأَ الْقُرْآنَ فَنَسِيَهُ، إِلَّا لَقِيَ اللَّهَ يَوْمَ يَلْقَاهُ وَهُوَ أَجْذَمُ" .

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي زِيَادٍ، عَنْ عِيسَى بْنِ فَائِدٍ، عَنْ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ الصَّامِتِ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَذَكَرَ مِثْلَهُ سَوَاءً .

---
